Random-restart hill-climbing DSRG search — results export
Generated: 2026-06-28T16:53:26
Result directories: rrhc_n64_results, rrhc_results
Files scanned: 3912

Method: random-restart steepest-descent hill climbing on the group ring
        difference-set equation (src/random_restart.g, RRHCkill).
        Each (group, parameter set) is given up to 300 random restarts.
        A 'FOUND' result is a connection set D with k elements such that
        e2(D^2 - t*1 - lambda*D - mu*(G - D - 1)) = 0 in Z[G].

========================================================================
Connection sets (GAP-loadable)
========================================================================

Each block reconstructs the group via SmallGroup(n, lib_id) and exposes
its generators as f1, f2, ... via AssignGeneratorVariables(G). The list
D is the connection set of the Cayley DSRG with parameters (n, k, t,
lambda, mu).

------------------------------------------------------------------------
# Parameters: n=64, k=17, t=8, lambda=3, mu=5
# Solutions found in 12 group(s) of order 64
------------------------------------------------------------------------

# n=64 lib_id=134  (k=17, t=8, lambda=3, mu=5)
G := SmallGroup(64, 134);;
AssignGeneratorVariables(G);;
D := [ f2*f5, f4*f5*f6, f1*f2*f5*f6, f3*f5*f6, f1*f3*f4*f5,  f1*f2*f3*f4*f6, f2*f3*f4, f1*f2*f6, f2*f3*f4*f5, f3*f4*f5*f6, f1*f4*f5, f1*f3*f5, f1*f2*f3*f4*f5*f6, f2, f1*f4*f6, f1*f4, f1 ];;

# n=64 lib_id=140  (k=17, t=8, lambda=3, mu=5)
G := SmallGroup(64, 140);;
